 succeeded in 0ms:
# Plow Sparkle Build Notes

This is the minimal build/release configuration for the Plow macOS updater.

## Build Settings Files

Committed:

- `app/Phoenix/Config/App.xcconfig`
- `app/Phoenix/Config/Local.xcconfig.example`

Ignored locally:

- `app/Phoenix/Config/Local.xcconfig`

`App.xcconfig` is the shared source of truth for updater-related Xcode build settings. It defines:

- `MARKETING_VERSION`
- `CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION`
- `SPARKLE_FEED_URL`
- `SPARKLE_PUBLIC_ED_KEY`

`App.xcconfig` ends with:

```xcconfig
#include? "Local.xcconfig"
```

That means local builds can override any of those settings without changing the committed project config.

## What Should Be Overridden Locally

Use `Local.xcconfig` only for local updater validation or ad hoc release testing.

Typical local overrides:

- `MARKETING_VERSION`
  - only for local `N -> N+1` upgrade tests
- `CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION`
  - only for local `N -> N+1` upgrade tests

The committed defaults should stay production-oriented.

## Secrets And Non-Repo State

These must not be committed:

- Sparkle private signing key
- Apple Developer ID signing credentials
- Apple notary profile credentials
- AWS credentials used to upload updater artifacts

These are safe to commit:

- Sparkle public key
- updater feed URL
- version/build defaults

## CI Requirements For A Real Sparkle Build

CI should treat the Git tag or release metadata as the source of truth for `MARKETING_VERSION`,
and inject a monotonic `CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION` at package time.

Required CI inputs:

1. `MARKETING_VERSION`
2. `CURRENT_PROJECT_VERSION`
3. access to the matching Sparkle private key in the macOS keychain used for `generate_appcast`
4. Apple Developer ID signing identity
5. Apple notarization profile/credentials
6. AWS credentials for publishing release artifacts

Recommended release order:

1. build signed `Plow.app`
2. `just app release`
   - uploads immutable versioned artifacts only:
   - `downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg`
   - `updates/Plow-<version>-<build>.zip`
   - `appcasts/Plow-<version>-<build>.xml`
3. optional local/manual validation
4. `just app promote <version> <build>`
   - updates stable pointers:
   - `Plow.dmg`
   - `appcast.xml`

## Current Scripts

Updater release scripts already in the repo:

- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-package-sparkle-update`
- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-stage-sparkle-feed`
- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-publish-sparkle-feed`
- `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-promote-release`

These handle:

- packaging a full Sparkle ZIP
- generating a staged appcast
- publishing explicit Sparkle feed files to S3
- promoting a versioned release to the stable DMG and appcast keys

## Local Override Flow

1. copy `app/Phoenix/Config/Local.xcconfig.example` to `app/Phoenix/Config/Local.xcconfig`
2. set a local version/build override if needed
3. build Plow

git add app/vm/manifest.toml app/Phoenix/Resources/runtime-manifest.json
git commit -m "bump(runtime): openclaw + camoufox"
```

This commit is what release CI later reads when it verifies the runtime S3 keys and packages the app.

## Step 6: Cut the App Release

Once the runtime update is merged to `main`, trigger the release-candidate workflow.

What happens in `build-release-candidate.yml`:

1. checks out `main`
2. verifies the two runtime S3 keys from `app/vm/manifest.toml`
3. runs `cd app && just release`
4. creates a versioned DMG and appcast
5. drafts a GitHub release tagged `deploy/app/v<version>-build.<build>`

`just release` does **not** upload runtime OCI tarballs. It only:

- regenerates `runtime-manifest.json` from `app/vm/manifest.toml`
- packages the signed/notarized app
- uploads the versioned DMG and appcast for that app release

The runtime artifact upload must already have happened before this point.

## Step 7: Promote the Published App Release

Publishing the GitHub draft release triggers `promote-app.yml`, which runs `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-promote-release`.

That script copies:

- `downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg` to `Plow.dmg`
- `downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg.sha256` to `Plow.dmg.sha256`
- `appcasts/Plow-<version>-<build>.xml` to `appcast.xml`

This promotion step affects the app installer/update feed only. It does **not** touch runtime OCI tarballs under `runtime/`.

## Verification Checklist

After `just runtime build`:

- `app/vm/manifest.toml` has the expected artifact names, shas, sizes, and git refs
- `app/Phoenix/Resources/runtime-manifest.json` matches the TOML entries
- both tarballs exist under `app/vm/output/`

     9	
    10	Mounts the given DMG, asserts the mounted volume is named "Plow" and has no
    11	.VolumeIcon.icns at its root, then detaches. Defaults to .build/Plow.dmg
    12	relative to the repo root.
    13	EOF
    14	}
    15	
    16	repo_root="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../../.." && pwd)"
    17	dmg_path="${repo_root}/.build/Plow.dmg"
    18	
    19	while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
    20	  case "$1" in
    21	    --dmg)
    22	      dmg_path="${2:-}"
    23	      shift 2
    24	      ;;
    25	    -h|--help)
    26	      usage
    27	      exit 0
    28	      ;;
    29	    *)
    30	      echo "error: unknown argument: $1" >&2
    31	      usage >&2
    32	      exit 1
    33	      ;;
    34	  esac
    35	done
    36	
    37	if [[ "${dmg_path}" != /* ]]; then
    38	  dmg_path="${repo_root}/${dmg_path}"
    39	fi
    40	
    41	[[ -f "${dmg_path}" ]] || { echo "error: DMG not found: ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    42	
    43	# Refuse to run when a Plow volume is already mounted: the new mountpoint
    44	# would be "Plow 1" / "Plow 2" / ..., which would mask a real regression in
    45	# the volume-name assertion below.
    46	mounted_plow_volumes="$(hdiutil info 2>/dev/null | grep -Eo '/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$' || true)"
    47	mounted_plow_volumes="$(printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" | sort -u)"
    48	if [[ -n "${mounted_plow_volumes}" ]]; then
    49	  echo "error: a Plow volume is already mounted; eject it before verifying:" >&2
    50	  printf '%s\n' "${mounted_plow_volumes}" >&2
    51	  exit 1
    52	fi
    53	
    54	mounted_volume=""
    55	cleanup() {
    56	  local rc=$?
    57	  if [[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]]; then
    58	    if [[ "${rc}" -eq 0 ]]; then
    59	      # Success path: detach failure (e.g. volume busy) must be fatal.
    60	      # Otherwise the next release retry trips ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume
    61	      # in plowd-beta-package-signed and aborts on a leaked mount.
    62	      if ! hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}"; then
    63	        echo "error: failed to detach ${mounted_volume} after successful verify" >&2
    64	        exit 1
    65	      fi
    66	    else
    67	      # Failure path: don't let detach noise mask the real error.
    68	      hdiutil detach "${mounted_volume}" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    69	    fi
    70	  fi
    71	  exit "${rc}"
    72	}
    73	trap cleanup EXIT
    74	
    75	attach_output="$(hdiutil attach "${dmg_path}" -nobrowse -readonly)"
    76	mounted_volume="$(printf '%s\n' "${attach_output}" | sed -n 's|.*\(/Volumes/.*\)$|\1|p' | head -n 1)"
    77	[[ -n "${mounted_volume}" ]] || { echo "error: failed to mount ${dmg_path}" >&2; exit 1; }
    78	
    79	volume_name="$(basename "${mounted_volume}")"
    80	[[ "${volume_name}" == "Plow" ]] || { echo "error: mounted volume name is '${volume_name}', expected 'Plow'" >&2; exit 1; }
    81	
    82	[[ ! -e "${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns" ]] || {
    83	  echo "error: ${mounted_volume}/.VolumeIcon.icns exists; PLO-29 regression: DMG ships a custom volume icon" >&2
    84	  exit 1
    85	}
    86	
    87	echo "ok: ${dmg_path} mounts as 'Plow' with no custom volume icon"

exec

    13	VALIDATE_PACKAGE_SCRIPT = REPO_ROOT / "app" / "plowd" / "scripts" / "plowd-validate-package"
    14	VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT = REPO_ROOT / "app" / "plowd" / "scripts" / "plowd-verify-dmg"

    16	PROVISION_SCRIPT = REPO_ROOT / "app" / "vm" / "provision-runtime.sh"
    17	PLOW_INSTALL_LIB = REPO_ROOT / "scripts" / "plow-install" / "lib.sh"

    20	def _provision_fake_bin(fake_bin: Path, systemctl_log: Path) -> None:
    21	    """Write stub commands sufficient to run provision-runtime.sh on macOS."""
    22	    stubs = {
    23	        # zstd just needs to be on PATH so the apt-get install branch is skipped
    24	        "zstd": "#!/bin/sh\n",
    25	        # sha256sum: hash stdin or file args, mimicking GNU coreutils behaviour
    26	        "sha256sum": textwrap.dedent("""\
    27	            #!/usr/bin/env python3
    28	            import hashlib, sys
    29	            from pathlib import Path
    30	            args = [a for a in sys.argv[1:] if a != "--"]
    31	            if args:
    32	                for arg in args:
    33	                    try:
    34	                        data = Path(arg).read_bytes()
    35	                        print(hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest() + "  " + arg)
    36	                    except FileNotFoundError:
    37	                        print(f"sha256sum: {arg}: No such file or directory", file=sys.stderr)
    38	                        sys.exit(1)
    39	            else:
    40	                data = sys.stdin.buffer.read()
    41	                print(hashlib.sha256(data).hexdigest() + "  -")
    42	            """),
    43	        # systemctl: log every invocation; always succeed
    44	        "systemctl": f'#!/bin/sh\necho "$@" >> "{systemctl_log}"\n',
    45	    }
    46	    for name, body in stubs.items():
    47	        p = fake_bin / name
    48	        p.write_text(body)
    49	        p.chmod(0o755)
    50

    52	def _run_provision(tmp_path: Path, fake_bin: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
    53	    unit_dir = tmp_path / "units"
    54	    unit_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    55	    libexec_dir = tmp_path / "libexec"
    56	    libexec_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    57	    return subprocess.run(
    58	        ["bash", str(PROVISION_SCRIPT)],
    59	        capture_output=True,
    60	        text=True,
    61	        env={
    62	            **subprocess.os.environ,
    63	            "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
    64	            "PLOW_UNIT_DIR": str(unit_dir),
    65	            "PLOW_LIBEXEC_DIR": str(libexec_dir),
    66	        },
    67	    )

    84	def test_provision_skips_containerd_restart_when_units_unchanged(tmp_path):
    85	    """containerd.service is not restarted when provision writes identical unit files."""

   254	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   255	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_rejects_dmg_shipping_volume_icon(tmp_path):
   256	    """PLO-29 artifact-level guard. Catches the failure mode that
   257	    ``test_signed_package_script_builds_ulfo_dmg_without_staging_ds_store``
   258	    cannot: a regression that re-attaches the DMG post-``hdiutil create``
   259	    and re-stages a custom volume icon at the final-image stage. We build
   260	    three real DMGs with hdiutil and assert plowd-verify-dmg accepts the
   261	    clean one and rejects each regression shape.
   262	
   263	    plowd-verify-dmg is wired into plowd-beta-package-signed between staple
   264	    and S3 upload, so a rejection here aborts ``just release`` before any
   265	    artifact ships."""
   266	    # Refuse to run if a real Plow volume is already mounted: the script
   267	    # bails on that and our assertions would tag the wrong failure mode.
   268	    info = subprocess.run(
   269	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   270	    )
   271	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   272	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   273	
   274	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   275	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   276	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   277	
   278	    def make_dmg(dmg_path: Path, *, volname: str) -> None:
   279	        subprocess.run(
   280	            [
   281	                "hdiutil", "create",
   282	                "-volname", volname,
   283	                "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   284	                "-ov",
   285	                "-format", "ULFO",
   286	                str(dmg_path),
   287	            ],
   288	            check=True, capture_output=True,
   289	        )
   290	
   291	    def run_verify(dmg_path: Path) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess[str]:
   292	        return subprocess.run(
   293	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg_path)],
   294	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   295	        )
   296	
   297	    # Happy path: clean Plow DMG with no .VolumeIcon must pass.
   298	    clean_dmg = tmp_path / "clean.dmg"
   299	    make_dmg(clean_dmg, volname="Plow")
   300	    ok = run_verify(clean_dmg)
   301	    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"clean DMG rejected: stdout={ok.stdout!r} stderr={ok.stderr!r}"
   302	
   303	    # Regression #1: someone re-introduces .VolumeIcon.icns at the volume root.
   304	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").write_text("fake-icns")
   305	    iconed_dmg = tmp_path / "iconed.dmg"
   306	    make_dmg(iconed_dmg, volname="Plow")
   307	    fail = run_verify(iconed_dmg)
   308	    assert fail.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG that ships .VolumeIcon.icns"
   309	    assert ".VolumeIcon.icns exists" in fail.stderr
   310	
   311	    # Regression #2: someone parameterizes -volname to something other than "Plow".
   312	    (stage / ".VolumeIcon.icns").unlink()
   313	    misnamed_dmg = tmp_path / "misnamed.dmg"
   314	    make_dmg(misnamed_dmg, volname="NotPlow")
   315	    fail2 = run_verify(misnamed_dmg)
   316	    assert fail2.returncode != 0, "verify-dmg accepted DMG with wrong volume name"
   317	    assert "expected 'Plow'" in fail2.stderr
   318	
   319	
   320	@pytest.mark.skipif(platform.system() != "Darwin", reason="hdiutil is macOS-only")
   321	def test_plowd_verify_dmg_propagates_detach_failure_on_success_path(tmp_path):
   322	    """Round-2: if `hdiutil detach` fails on the success path (e.g. the
   323	    volume is busy), plowd-verify-dmg must exit non-zero. The previous
   324	    `|| true` swallowed the failure and returned 0, leaking /Volumes/Plow,
   325	    which then tripped ensure_no_mounted_plow_volume on the next release
   326	    retry. This test injects an `hdiutil` wrapper whose `detach` always
   327	    fails and asserts the script surfaces it."""
   328	    info = subprocess.run(
   329	        ["hdiutil", "info"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   330	    )
   331	    if re.search(r"/Volumes/Plow( [0-9]+)?$", info.stdout, re.MULTILINE):
   332	        pytest.skip("a Plow volume is mounted; eject it before running this test")
   333	
   334	    stage = tmp_path / "stage"
   335	    (stage / "Plow.app").mkdir(parents=True)
   336	    (stage / "Plow.app" / "PlaceHolder").write_text("dummy")
   337	    dmg = tmp_path / "Plow.dmg"
   338	    subprocess.run(
   339	        [
   340	            "hdiutil", "create",
   341	            "-volname", "Plow",
   342	            "-srcfolder", str(stage),
   343	            "-ov",
   344	            "-format", "ULFO",
   345	            str(dmg),
   346	        ],
   347	        check=True, capture_output=True,
   348	    )
   349	
   350	    real_hdiutil = subprocess.run(
   351	        ["which", "hdiutil"], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True,
   352	    ).stdout.strip()
   353	    fake_bin = tmp_path / "bin"
   354	    fake_bin.mkdir()
   355	    wrapper = fake_bin / "hdiutil"
   356	    wrapper.write_text(
   357	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\n"
   358	        f'if [[ "$1" == "detach" ]]; then\n'
   359	        f'  echo "fake: detach failure (test injection)" >&2\n'
   360	        f'  exit 16\n'
   361	        f'fi\n'
   362	        f'exec "{real_hdiutil}" "$@"\n'
   363	    )
   364	    wrapper.chmod(0o755)
   365	
   366	    try:
   367	        result = subprocess.run(
   368	            [str(VERIFY_DMG_SCRIPT), "--dmg", str(dmg)],
   369	            capture_output=True, text=True,
   370	            env={
   371	                **subprocess.os.environ,
   372	                "PATH": f"{fake_bin}:{subprocess.os.environ['PATH']}",
   373	            },
   374	        )
   375	        assert result.returncode != 0, (
   376	            f"verify-dmg returned 0 despite detach failure; mount leaked.\n"
   377	            f"stdout={result.stdout!r}\nstderr={result.stderr!r}"
   378	        )
   379	        assert "failed to detach" in result.stderr, (
   380	            f"expected 'failed to detach' in stderr, got: {result.stderr!r}"
   381	        )
   382	    finally:
   383	        # Real hdiutil to clean up the leaked mount the wrapper refused to release.
   384	        subprocess.run(
   385	            [real_hdiutil, "detach", "/Volumes/Plow"],
   386	            capture_output=True,
   387	        )
   388

   442	def test_build_runtime_artifacts_rebuilds_when_manifest_version_bumps_but_tarball_is_stale(tmp_path):
   443	    app_root = tmp_path / "app"
   444	    scripts_dir = app_root / "scripts"
   445	    lib_dir = scripts_dir / "lib"
   446	    vm_dir = app_root / "vm"
   447	    output_dir = vm_dir / "output"
   448	    scripts_dir.mkdir(parents=True)
   449	    lib_dir.mkdir(parents=True)
   450	    output_dir.mkdir(parents=True)
   451	
   452	    (scripts_dir / "build-runtime-artifacts.sh").write_text(
   453	        (REPO_ROOT / "app" / "scripts" / "build-runtime-artifacts.sh").read_text(encoding="utf-8"),
   454	        encoding="utf-8",
   455	    )
   456	    (scripts_dir / "build-runtime-artifacts.sh").chmod(0o755)
   457	    (lib_dir / "git-ref.sh").write_text(
   458	        "#!/usr/bin/env bash\ncompute_git_ref() { printf '%s\\n' same123; }\n",
   459	        encoding="utf-8",
   460	    )
   461	    (lib_dir / "git-ref.sh").chmod(0o755)
   462	
   463	    manifest_path = vm_dir / "manifest.toml"
   464	    manifest_path.write_text(
   465	        textwrap.dedent(
   466	            """
   467	            openclaw_version = "2026.4.22"
   468	            openclaw_artifact = "openclaw-agent-2026.4.21.same123.tar.zst"
   469	            openclaw_sha256 = "old-openclaw"
   470	            openclaw_size = 1
   471	            openclaw_git_ref = "same123"
   472	            camoufox_image_version = "135.0.1-beta.25"
   473	            camoufox_image_artifact = "camoufox-135.0.1-beta.24.same123.tar.zst"
   474	            camoufox_image_sha256 = "old-camoufox"
   475	            camoufox_image_size = 1
   476	            camoufox_image_git_ref = "same123"
   477	            """
   478	        ).strip()
   479	        + "\n",
   480	        encoding="utf-8",
   481	    )
   482	
   483	    stale_openclaw = output_dir / "openclaw-agent-2026.4.21.same123.tar.zst"
   484	    stale_camoufox = output_dir / "camoufox-135.0.1-beta.24.same123.tar.zst"
   485	    stale_openclaw.write_text("stale-openclaw\n", encoding="utf-8")
   486	    stale_camoufox.write_text("stale-camoufox\n", encoding="utf-8")
   487	
   488	    build_log = tmp_path / "build.log"
   489	    _write_fake_runtime_child_builder(
   490	        scripts_dir / "build-agent-image.sh",
   491	        build_log,
   492	        "openclaw",
   493	        "openclaw_artifact",
   494	        "rebuilt-openclaw\n",
   495	    )
   496	    _write_fake_runtime_child_builder(
   497	        scripts_dir / "build-camoufox-image.sh",
   498	        build_log,
   499	        "camoufox",
   500	        "camoufox_image_artifact",
   501	        "rebuilt-camoufox\n",
   502	    )
   503	
   504	    result = subprocess.run(
   505	        [str(scripts_dir / "build-runtime-artifacts.sh")],
   506	        capture_output=True,
   507	        text=True,
   508	        cwd=app_root,
   509	    )
   510	
   511	    assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
   512	    assert build_log.read_text(encoding="utf-8").splitlines() == ["openclaw", "camoufox"]
   513	    assert stale_openclaw.read_text(encoding="utf-8") == "rebuilt-openclaw\n"
   514	    assert stale_camoufox.read_text(encoding="utf-8") == "rebuilt-camoufox\n"

   517	def _create_minimal_valid_app_bundle(app_bundle: Path) -> None:
   518	    contents_root = app_bundle / "Contents"
   519	    macos_root = contents_root / "MacOS"
   520	    runtime_root = app_bundle / "Contents" / "Resources" / "runtime"
   521	    vm_root = app_bundle / "Contents" / "Resources" / "vm"
   522	    info_plist = contents_root / "Info.plist"
   523	    macos_binary = macos_root / "Plow"
   524	    macos_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   525	    info_plist.write_text(
   526	        """<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
   527	<!DOCTYPE plist PUBLIC "-//Apple//DTD PLIST 1.0//EN" "http://www.apple.com/DTDs/PropertyList-1.0.dtd">
   528	<plist version="1.0">
   529	<dict>
   530	    <key>CFBundleName</key>
   531	    <string>Plow</string>
   532	    <key>CFBundleShortVersionString</key>
   533	    <string>0.1.0</string>
   534	    <key>CFBundleVersion</key>
   535	    <string>1</string>
   536	    <key>SUFeedURL</key>
   537	    <string>https://example.test/appcast.xml</string>
   538	    <key>SUPublicEDKey</key>
   539	    <string>test-public-key</string>
   540	</dict>
   541	</plist>
   542	""",
   543	        encoding="utf-8",
   544	    )
   545	    macos_binary.write_text("#!/bin/sh\nexit 0\n", encoding="utf-8")
   546	    macos_binary.chmod(0o755)
   547	    # python3 must be a real interpreter for plowd-validate-package's manifest check
   548	    python_bin = runtime_root / "python" / "bin" / "python3"
   549	    python_bin.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   550	    python_bin.symlink_to(sys.executable)
   551	    required_files = [
   552	        runtime_root / "plowd",
   553	        runtime_root / "scripts" / "plowd-dashboard",
   554	        runtime_root / "scripts" / "plowd-vm-shell",
   555	        runtime_root / "site-packages" / ".keep",
   556	        # plowd-validate-package now requires plowd-*.dist-info/METADATA in
   557	        # site-packages so the daemon can resolve importlib.metadata.version.
   558	        runtime_root / "site-packages" / "plowd-0.1.1.dist-info" / "METADATA",
   559	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "plugins" / "guard" / ".keep",
   560	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "plugins" / "plow-cli" / "index.js",
   561	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "plugins" / "plow-cli" / "openclaw.plugin.json",
   562	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "plugins" / "plow-cli" / "package.json",
   563	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-imessage" / "openclaw.plugin.json",
   564	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-imessage" / "package.json",
   565	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-imessage" / "dist" / "index.js",
   566	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-imessage" / "dist" / "openclaw.plugin.json",
   567	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-imessage" / "node_modules" / "ws" / "package.json",
   568	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-slack" / "package.json",
   569	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-slack" / "dist" / "index.js",
   570	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-slack" / "dist" / "openclaw.plugin.json",
   571	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "channels" / "plow-slack" / "node_modules" / "ws" / "package.json",
   572	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "templates" / "workspace" / "AGENTS.md",
   573	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "templates" / "workspace" / "IDENTITY.md",
   574	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "templates" / "workspace" / "README.md",
   575	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "templates" / "workspace" / "USER.md",
   576	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "templates" / "workspace" / "skills" / "browser-usage" / "SKILL.md",
   577	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "templates" / "workspace" / "skills" / "plow-calendar" / "SKILL.md",
   578	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "templates" / "workspace" / "skills" / "plow-file-discovery" / "SKILL.md",
   579	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "templates" / "workspace" / "skills" / "plow-vip-contacts" / "SKILL.md",
   580	        runtime_root / "openclaw" / "marketplace" / "marketplace.html",
   581	        runtime_root / "cli-packages" / "plow" / "__init__.py",
   582	        runtime_root / "cli-packages" / "python" / "bin" / "python3.12",
   583	        runtime_root / "cli-packages" / "bin" / "plow",
   584	        runtime_root / "lima.yaml",
   585	        runtime_root / "provision-runtime.sh",
   586	    ]
   587	    for file_path in required_files:
   588	        file_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   589	        file_path.write_text("placeholder")
   590	    # runtime-manifest.json is validated by plowd-validate-package
   591	    manifest_path = contents_root / "Resources" / "runtime-manifest.json"
   592	    manifest_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   593	    manifest_path.write_text(
   594	        '{"artifacts": [{"name": "openclaw", "version": "1.0", "url": "https://example.test/openclaw.tar.zst", "sha256": "abc", "size": 1, "gitRef": ""}, {"name": "camoufox", "version": "1.0", "url": "https://example.test/camoufox.tar.zst", "sha256": "bcd", "size": 1, "gitRef": ""}]}',
   595	        encoding="utf-8",
   596	    )

   599	def test_validate_package_rejects_bundle_missing_plowd_dist_info(tmp_path):
   600	    """A packaged runtime that exists structurally but lacks plowd-*.dist-info/
   601	    is the exact regression #478 shape: site-packages/ is present, all files
   602	    pass the existence check, but plowd dies at import with PackageNotFoundError
   603	    because importlib.metadata can't find the metadata."""
   604	    app_bundle = tmp_path / "Plow.app"
   605	    _create_minimal_valid_app_bundle(app_bundle)
   606	
   607	    # Sanity: the unmodified bundle passes validation.
   608	    ok = subprocess.run(
   609	        [str(VALIDATE_PACKAGE_SCRIPT), "--app-bundle", str(app_bundle), "--mode", "offline"],
   610	        capture_output=True,
   611	        text=True,
   612	    )
   613	    assert ok.returncode == 0, f"baseline bundle should validate cleanly, got: {ok.stderr}"
   614	
   615	    # Remove the dist-info; site-packages/ itself stays so this isn't caught
   616	    # by the existing required_runtime_paths loop.
   617	    dist_info = (
   618	        app_bundle / "Contents" / "Resources" / "runtime"
   619	        / "site-packages" / "plowd-0.1.1.dist-info"
   620	    )
   621	    import shutil
   622	    shutil.rmtree(dist_info)
   623	
   624	    fail = subprocess.run(
   625	        [str(VALIDATE_PACKAGE_SCRIPT), "--app-bundle", str(app_bundle), "--mode", "offline"],
   626	        capture_output=True,
   627	        text=True,
   628	    )
   629	    assert fail.returncode != 0, "validate-package must reject a bundle missing plowd dist-info"
   630	    assert "plowd-*.dist-info" in fail.stderr, (
   631	        f"error message should mention the missing dist-info; got stderr:\n{fail.stderr}"
   632	    )
   633	
   634	
   635	def test_validate_package_pins_plowd_dist_info_check():
   636	    """Static guard so a future deletion of the dist-info check in
   637	    plowd-validate-package surfaces here, not as a packaged-app crash."""
   638	    validate_script = VALIDATE_PACKAGE_SCRIPT.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
   639	    assert "plowd-*.dist-info/METADATA" in validate_script, (
   640	        "plowd-validate-package must check for plowd-*.dist-info/METADATA so "
   641	        "regression #478 can't ship as a structurally-valid-but-unbootable bundle"
   642	    )

   645	def test_stage_runtime_installs_plowd_dist_info():
   646	    """plowd's `importlib.metadata.version("plowd")` calls need `plowd-*.dist-info/`
   647	    on sys.path. The rsync of the source tree into `${stage_dir}/plowd` doesn't
   648	    include metadata, so plowd-stage-runtime must explicitly install plowd into
   649	    site-packages alongside the external deps so the dist-info is present.
   650	    Without this, packaged apps die at import with PackageNotFoundError before
   651	    binding the HTTP port (regression #478)."""
   652	    stage_script = (
   653	        REPO_ROOT / "app" / "plowd" / "scripts" / "plowd-stage-runtime"
   654	    ).read_text(encoding="utf-8")
   655	
   656	    # Whitespace-tolerant: pin the unique combination of flags that identifies
   657	    # the dist-info install (--no-deps + ${project_root}) without locking the
   658	    # script to a specific line-continuation/indent style.
   659	    assert re.search(
   660	        r'uv pip install\b[^\n]*'
   661	        r'(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
   662	        r'--target\s+"\$\{stage_dir\}/site-packages"'
   663	        r'[^\n]*(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
   664	        r'--no-deps'
   665	        r'[^\n]*(?:\\\s*\n[^\n]*)*'
   666	        r'"\$\{project_root\}"',
   667	        stage_script,
   668	    ), (
   669	        "plowd-stage-runtime must `uv pip install --no-deps` plowd into "
   670	        "${stage_dir}/site-packages so the daemon's importlib.metadata.version"
   671	        "('plowd') call resolves"
   672	    )
   673

   949	import json
   950	import os
   951	from pathlib import Path
   952	import shutil
   953	import sys
   954	
   955	
   956	log_dir = Path(os.environ["FAKE_LOG_DIR"])
   957	map_path = log_dir / "hdiutil-map.json"
   958	if map_path.exists():
   959	    image_map = json.loads(map_path.read_text())
   960	else:
   961	    image_map = {}
   962	
   963	
   964	def save_map() -> None:
   965	    map_path.write_text(json.dumps(image_map))
   966	
   967	
   968	def image_dir_for(image_path: str) -> Path:
   969	    digest = hashlib.sha256(image_path.encode()).hexdigest()
   970	    return log_dir / "images" / digest
   971	
   972	
   973	def copy_tree(src: Path, dest: Path) -> None:
   974	    if dest.exists():
   975	        shutil.rmtree(dest)
   976	    dest.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   977	    shutil.copytree(src, dest, symlinks=True)
   978	
   979	
   980	def find_value(flag: str, args: list[str]) -> str:
   981	    return args[args.index(flag) + 1]
   982	
   983	
   984	with (log_dir / "hdiutil.log").open("a") as fh:
   985	    fh.write(" ".join(sys.argv[1:]) + "\\n")
   986	
   987	command = sys.argv[1]
   988	args = sys.argv[2:]
   989	
   990	if command == "create":
   991	    srcfolder = Path(find_value("-srcfolder", args))
   992	    output = Path(args[-1])
   993	    output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   994	    output.write_text("fake dmg")
   995	    captured = log_dir / "captured-srcfolder"
   996	    copy_tree(srcfolder, captured)
   997	    image_dir = image_dir_for(str(output))
   998	    copy_tree(srcfolder, image_dir)
   999	    image_map[str(output)] = str(image_dir)
  1000	    save_map()
  1001	    sys.exit(0)
  1002	
  1003	if command == "attach":
  1004	    image = next(arg for arg in args if not arg.startswith("-"))
  1005	    mount_dir = Path("/Volumes") / f"fake-{hashlib.sha256(image.encode()).hexdigest()[:12]}"
  1006	    image_map[f"mount::{mount_dir}"] = image
  1007	    save_map()
  1008	    print(f"/dev/disk9s1 Apple_APFS {mount_dir}")
  1009	    sys.exit(0)
  1010	
  1011	if command == "detach":
  1012	    mount_dir = Path(args[0])
  1013	    sys.exit(0)
  1014	
  1015	if command == "convert":
  1016	    source_image = next(arg for arg in args if not arg.startswith("-"))
  1017	    output = Path(find_value("-o", args))
  1018	    output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

  1022	    copy_tree(source_dir, output_dir)
  1023	    image_map[str(output)] = str(output_dir)

 succeeded in 0ms:
   198	Once the runtime update is merged to `main`, trigger the release-candidate workflow.
   199	
   200	What happens in `build-release-candidate.yml`:
   201	
   202	1. checks out `main`
   203	2. verifies the two runtime S3 keys from `app/vm/manifest.toml`
   204	3. runs `cd app && just release`
   205	4. creates a versioned DMG and appcast
   206	5. drafts a GitHub release tagged `deploy/app/v<version>-build.<build>`
   207	
   208	`just release` does **not** upload runtime OCI tarballs. It only:
   209	
   210	- regenerates `runtime-manifest.json` from `app/vm/manifest.toml`
   211	- packages the signed/notarized app
   212	- uploads the versioned DMG and appcast for that app release
   213	
   214	The runtime artifact upload must already have happened before this point.
   215	
   216	## Step 7: Promote the Published App Release
   217	
   218	Publishing the GitHub draft release triggers `promote-app.yml`, which runs `app/plowd/scripts/plowd-promote-release`.
   219	
   220	That script copies:
   221	
   222	- `downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg` to `Plow.dmg`
   223	- `downloads/Plow-<version>-<build>.dmg.sha256` to `Plow.dmg.sha256`
   224	- `appcasts/Plow-<version>-<build>.xml` to `appcast.xml`
   225	
   226	This promotion step affects the app installer/update feed only. It does **not** touch runtime OCI tarballs under `runtime/`.

[private]
channel-install:
    cd ../openclaw/channels/plow-imessage && npm install

# Strict lockfile install (for CI and version-bump validation). Fails if
# package-lock.json is out of sync with package.json — which is exactly
# what you want when catching accidental drift.
[private]
channel-install-ci:
    cd ../openclaw/channels/plow-imessage && npm ci

[private]
channel-build:
    cd ../openclaw/channels/plow-imessage && npm run build

[private]
channel-watch:
    cd ../openclaw/channels/plow-imessage && npm run build:watch

[private]
channel-compile: channel-build

[private]
channel-typecheck:
    cd ../openclaw/channels/plow-imessage && npx tsc --noEmit

[private]
channel-test:
    cd ../openclaw/channels/plow-imessage && npm test

[private]
channel-check: channel-install channel-build channel-typecheck channel-test

# CI entry point: strict install, typecheck first (cheapest failure signal),
# then build, then tests. Called from .github/workflows/test.yml.
[private]
channel-check-ci: channel-install-ci channel-typecheck channel-build channel-test

codex
## [architecture] findings

### Surveyed
- Release flow boundary: `just app release` is the documented point that packages and uploads the versioned DMG — see Finding 1
- DMG staging path: custom `.VolumeIcon.icns` staging and UDRW custom-icon mutation are removed — clean
- Artifact verifier placement: verifier runs after staple and before S3 upload — see Finding 1
- macOS CI lane: plowd tests now run where real `hdiutil` exists — clean
- Deleted DMG volume icon asset: removes an orphaned release asset rather than adding another conditional path — clean

### Finding 1 — medium
The release verifier is not actually a single mandatory release contract because `PLOW_SKIP_DMG_VERIFY=1` skips it in the production packaging script. The documented release flow says `just app release` packages and uploads the versioned DMG (`docs/phoenix-sparkle-build.md:73`, `docs/vm-publish.md:208`), and this PR’s intent is to block releases that ship the confusing custom volume icon. But line 299 lets any inherited release environment bypass the guard, and the script still uploads at lines 315-316. Broken-Glass Test, Concise Code, and Fail-Fast all point the same way here: removing the env bypass reduces branch count and makes the verifier the one release path.
Files: app/plowd/scripts/plowd-beta-package-signed:299, app/plowd/scripts/plowd-beta-package-signed:315, docs/vm-publish.md:208
tokens used
